  "article_text": [
    "for every plane diagram of an oriented link @xmath4 , khovanov s link homology theory  @xcite yields a chain complex @xmath5 of graded vector spaces whose graded euler characteristic agrees with the jones polynomial of the link . this construction can be seen as a categorification of the unnormalized jones polynomial , replacing a polynomial in one indeterminate @xmath6 by a chain complex of graded vector spaces .",
    "the coefficients of the polynomial arise as the dimensions of the homogeneous components of the graded homology groups of the chain complex in such a way that the degree corresponds to the power of @xmath6 .    if two link diagrams are related by a reidemeister move , the corresponding chain complexes of graded vector spaces are homotopy equivalent , and so their homology groups are isomorphic as graded vector spaces .",
    "this of course implies that their graded euler characteristics and thereby their unnormalized jones polynomials agree , but in general the homology groups contain more information about the link than does the jones polynomial .",
    "indeed , bar - natan and wehrli  @xcite have shown that there are knots and links that have the same jones polynomial , but which can be distinguished by their khovanov homology .",
    "the construction of khovanov s chain complex heavily relies on a @xmath0-dimensional topological quantum field theory ( tqft ) .",
    "the fact that the boundary of a cobordism is a closed manifold , naturally restricts the construction to links rather than arbitrary tangles .",
    "the purpose of the present article is to overcome this limitation . in the remainder of the introduction",
    ", we give a brief overview of the present article , addressed to the experts .",
    "the reader who is familiar with the details of khovanov s definition  @xcite and with bar - natan s work on the extension from links to tangles  @xcite , should be able to understand the key ideas of our work just from reading the introduction .",
    "the reader who is not familiar with all the details , is invited to have a brief look at the introduction in order to get a first impression , and can then work though the material step by step starting from section  [ sect_prelim ] .",
    "let @xmath4 be a plane diagram of an oriented link with @xmath7 positive crossings @xmath8 and @xmath9 negative ones @xmath10 , @xmath11 .",
    "the kauffman bracket @xmath12 from which one can compute the unnormalized jones polynomial @xmath13 $ ] , can be recursively defined for @xmath6 in the normalized polynomial @xmath14 . ] as follows : @xmath15 for every crossing @xmath16 , each of the two smoothings , the @xmath17-smoothing @xmath18 and the @xmath19-smoothing @xmath20 , give a contribution to the kauffman bracket , with a different sign and a different power of @xmath6 .",
    "for the link diagram @xmath4 with @xmath21 crossings , there are @xmath22 smoothings , labeled by subsets @xmath23 where @xmath24 if the @xmath25-th crossing is resolved by the @xmath19-smoothing and @xmath26 if it is resolved by the @xmath17-smoothing .",
    "we denote by @xmath27 , @xmath28 , the diagrams associated with the @xmath22 smoothings of @xmath4 .",
    "each @xmath29 is free of crossings and therefore forms a disjoint union of a finite number of circles in @xmath30 .    a crucial ingredient for the construction of khovanov s chain complex is the following collection of cobordisms between these diagrams .",

    "\\psline[linestyle = dotted , dotsep=2pt](0.2,1.52)(0.2,0.6 )    \\psbezier[linestyle = dotted , dotsep=2pt](0.2,0.6)(0.7,0.4)(2.2,0.4)(2.5,0.55 )    \\psline[linestyle = dotted , dotsep=2pt](2.5,0.55)(2.7,0.6 ) } } \\end{pspicture } \\end{aligned}\\ ] ] with the @xmath17-smoothing @xmath20 as the source ( at the top of the diagram ) and the @xmath19-smoothing @xmath18 as the target ( at the bottom ) .",
    "then one uses a @xmath0-dimensional tqft ,  a symmetric monoidal functor @xmath37 from the category @xmath38 of @xmath0-dimensional cobordisms to the category @xmath39 of vector spaces over some fixed field @xmath40 , in order to turn the cobordism into a linear map between vector spaces .",
    "the chain groups of khovanov s chain complex are constructed from the vector spaces @xmath41 , @xmath28 , and the differentials from the linear maps @xmath42 , @xmath31 , @xmath32 . for more details , see section  [ sec_tangle ] below , and for the full explanation of how khovanov s theory is related to the jones polynomial , we refer to  @xcite .    the category of @xmath0-dimensional tqfts ,  the category @xmath43 of symmetric monoidal functors @xmath44 and monoidal natural transformations , is equivalent as a symmetric monoidal category to the category of commutative frobenius algebras over @xmath40  @xcite .",

    "composition of morphisms corresponds to putting the building blocks of   on top of each other .",
    "the tensor product of morphisms is the disjoint union of cobordisms . if we denote by @xmath47 the vector space associated with a single circle , the functor @xmath48 yields linear maps @xmath49 , @xmath50 , @xmath51 , and @xmath52 for these cobordisms .",
    "the relations among the morphisms of @xmath38 are such that @xmath53 forms a commutative frobenius algebra .",
    "khovanov s original choice of frobenius algebra , called @xmath54 $ ] in  @xcite , over the commutative ring @xmath55 $ ] , is such that one gets a chain complex of graded modules and a categorification of the jones polynomial .",
    "his tqft is actually a functor @xmath56 . in this article",
    ", we restrict ourselves to the case @xmath57 (  @xcite ) and to algebras over a field @xmath40 . with this restriction ,",
    "khovanov s commutative",
    "frobenius algebra forms the special case @xmath58 , @xmath59 of the following definition :    [ def_khovanov ] let @xmath40 be a field and @xmath60 .",
    "@xmath61 denotes the algebra @xmath62/(x^2-hx - t)$ ] equipped with the structure of a commutative frobenius algebra @xmath63 which is given in the basis @xmath64 by @xmath65 , @xmath66 , @xmath67 , @xmath68 , @xmath69 , @xmath70 , @xmath71 , @xmath72 , and @xmath73 .",
    "several results below depend on the characteristic of @xmath40 . while khovanov originally studied the case @xmath58 , @xmath59 , lee  @xcite considered @xmath58 , @xmath74 , and bar - natan  @xcite studied @xmath75 , @xmath59 .",
    "below , we refer to @xmath76 as _",
    "khovanov s _ , to @xmath77 as _ lee s _ , and to @xmath78 as _ bar - natan s _ frobenius algebra .",
    "the link homology theory associated with khovanov s frobenius algebra is known to categorify the jones polynomial , a _ quantum invariant _ of links . in some cases",
    ", the other two link homology theories are related to _",
    "classical invariants _ of links : both lee s theory in characteristic @xmath17  @xcite and bar - natan s theory in characteristic @xmath0  @xcite categorify combinatorial expressions involving linking numbers .",
    "bar - natan  @xcite has presented sufficient ( but not necessary ) conditions for tqfts to yield link homology theories .",
    "these can be stated in topological and in algebraic terms as follows :    [ def_barnatancond ]    1 .",

    "a commutative frobenius algebra @xmath53 is said to _",
    "satisfy bar - natan s conditions _",
    "if @xmath80    the frobenius algebra @xmath61 of definition  [ def_khovanov ] satisfies bar - natan s conditions for all @xmath60 .",
    "khovanov  @xcite has classified the frobenius algebras that give rise to link homology theories .",
    "the algebra @xmath61 of definition  [ def_khovanov ] is a specialization of @xmath81 of  @xcite to a field @xmath40 and to @xmath60 .",
    "the classification includes examples , for instance khovanov s @xmath54 $ ] without evaluation at @xmath82 , called @xmath83 in  @xcite , which do not satisfy all of bar - natan s conditions   to  . in the present article",
    ", we restrict ourselves to frobenius algebras that do satisfy these conditions .",
    "we wish to extend these link homology theories from links to tangles . for tangles ,",
    "the diagrams @xmath84 corresponding to the smoothings would consist not only of circles , but rather of circles and arcs .",
    "khovanov has already remarked in  @xcite that one would need an extended @xmath0-dimensional tqft in which the cobordisms are generalized to suitable manifolds with corners .    even without an extended tqft ,",
    "there have been two workarounds .",
    "khovanov  @xcite considers tangles with an even number of points both for the source and the target of the tangle , so - called _ even tangles _ , and presents a definition in which the tangle homology is reduced to his link homology by closing the open ends of the tangles in all possible ways and taking the sum over the resulting expressions for the links .",
    "he thus obtains a tangle homology theory only for even tangles , but it is still possible to tell which expression this construction categorifies .",
    "bar - natan  @xcite works with formal linear combinations of manifolds with corners .",
    "as long as one stays in this topological setting , called the ` picture world ' , one has good composition laws for tangles , but bar - natan still relies on a tqft and can therefore translate from topology to algebra only for links ,  after all open ends have been closed .",
    "the following two questions remain to be answered and form the subject of the present article :    1 .",
    "how does one define a homology theory for arbitrary oriented tangles , using only algebraic as opposed to topological ` picture world ' constructions ? 2 .",
    "which algebraic operation corresponds to the composition of tangles ?",
    "in particular , we wish to understand which algebraic data to assign to a single arc ( @xmath85 ) so that one can take a disjoint union of two such arcs ( @xmath86 ) , then glue on a cap ( @xmath87 ) and a cup ( @xmath88 ) in order to obtain a circle in such a way that both operations , disjoint union ( tensor product ) and gluing ( composition ) have a correspondence on the algebraic side . if we write @xmath89 for the algebraic data associated with a tangle diagram @xmath90 , this means that : @xmath91 this can not be done by khovanov s method  @xcite since a single arc is not an even tangle , and it can not be done by bar - natan s method  @xcite since there one can translate from topology to algebra only for links , but not for a single arc which forms a proper tangle .",
    "a further limitation of the existing link homology theories is the following .",
    "recall that the cobordisms @xmath34 of   are the disjoint union of either @xmath92 {          \\psbezier(1.5,2.5)(1.5,1.1)(.4,1.6)(.5,0 )          \\psbezier(.5,0)(.4,-.25)(-.4,-.25)(-.5,0 )          \\psbezier(-0.5,0)(-.4,1.6)(-1.5,1.1)(-1.5,2.5 )          \\psline(-.5,2.5 )          \\psbezier(-.5,2.5)(-.6,1.5)(0.6,1.5)(.5,2.5 )          \\psline(1.5,2.5 )      }       \\psellipse[fillcolor = lightgray , fillstyle = gradient ,          gradbegin = lightgray , gradend = gray , gradmidpoint=1,gradangle=110](-1,2.5)(.5,.2 )      \\psellipse[fillcolor = lightgray , fillstyle = gradient ,          gradbegin = lightgray , gradend = gray , gradmidpoint=1,gradangle=110](1,2.5)(.5,.2 )        \\begin{psclip } {   \\pspolygon[linestyle = none](.5,0)(.5,.3)(-.5,.3)(-.5,0)(.5,0 )   }   \\psellipse[linestyle = dotted](0,0)(.5,0.2 )   \\end{psclip }   } } \\end{pspicture}$ ] or @xmath93 {          \\psbezier(1.5,0)(1.5,1.4)(.4,.9)(.5,2.5 )          \\psline(-0.5,2.5 )          \\psbezier(-0.5,2.5)(-.4,.9)(-1.5,1.4)(-1.5,0 )          \\psbezier(-1.5,0)(-1.4,-.25)(-.6,-.25)(-.5,0 )          \\psbezier(-.5,0)(-.6,1)(0.6,1)(.5,0 )          \\psbezier(.5,0)(.6,-.25)(1.4,-.25)(1.5,0 )      }    \\psellipse[fillcolor = lightgray , fillstyle = gradient ,          gradbegin = lightgray , gradend = gray , gradmidpoint=1,gradangle=110](0,2.5)(.5,.2 ) \\begin{psclip } {   \\pspolygon[linestyle = none](1.5,0)(1.5,.3)(-1.5,.3)(-1.5,0)(1.5,0 )   }   \\psellipse[linestyle = dotted](1,0)(.5,0.2 )   \\psellipse[linestyle = dotted](-1,0)(.5,0.2 )   \\end{psclip }   } } \\end{pspicture}$ ] and a number of cylinders over circles . in order to decide which one of the two cobordisms with critical point of index @xmath19",

    "open - closed cobordisms are composed by gluing them along their _ black _ boundaries .",
    "an open - closed tqft is a symmetric monoidal functor @xmath106 . if we denote by @xmath107 the vector space associated with a single arc and by @xmath108 the vector space for a single circle , then the relations of @xmath95 are precisely the moore ",
    "segal relations  @xcite .",
    "they imply that @xmath109 forms what we call a knowledgeable frobenius algebra ,  that @xmath110 is a symmetric frobenius algebra , that @xmath111 is a commutative frobenius algebra , and that some additional conditions on @xmath112 and @xmath113 hold . for the details ,",
    "we refer to section  [ sect_kfrob ] below .    from bar - natan s work  @xcite and from his purely topological proof of the invariance of his tangle homology under reidemeister moves ,",
    "it is immediately obvious that an open - closed tqft is just the appropriate tool for turning bar - natan s topological setup into an algebraic tangle homology theory . what remains to be done",
    "is to find knowledgeable frobenius algebras @xmath109 and thereby open - closed tqfts that satisfy the conditions   to  .",
    "we present examples of such knowledgeable frobenius algebras @xmath109 for which @xmath114 ( definition  [ def_khovanov ] ) and for which the resulting tangle homology theories reduce to the link homology theories of khovanov , lee , and bar - natan when they are evaluated for links .",
    "this resolves the first issue , namely to find homology theories for arbitrary oriented tangles ( see theorem  [ thm_reidemeister ] below ) .    if we wish to extend khovanov s frobenius algebra     "khovanov s frobenius algebra @xmath76 in any characteristic and lee s frobenius algebra in characteristic @xmath0 are not semisimple and both fail to yield a tangle homology theory that is well behaved under tangle composition defined in this way .",
    "this is no surprise .",
    "the non - semisimplicity of khovanov s frobenius algebra is closely related to the fact that it can detect _ global _ properties of the tangle that can not be easily computed _ locally _ ,  from the constituents of the tangle .    but",
    "does this mean that our method of composing tangles rules out the most interesting example , namely khovanov s ?",
    "no , it does not .",
    "there is still a way out .",
    "it is known , for example , from the work of lee and rasmussen  @xcite and of turner  @xcite that for links , the chain complex and homology for khovanov s frobenius algebra can be recovered from a filtration on the chain complex of lee or bar - natan , respectively , by computing the @xmath160- and @xmath161-pages of a certain spectral sequence .",
    "when we extend this method of computing khovanov s chain complex from links to tangles , there are additional conditions to satisfy , and an analogous spectral sequence only exists over fields of finite characteristic ( see example  [ ex_barnatan ] , theorem  [ thm_sskfrob ] and examples  [ ex_filtered ] to  [ ex_filtered3 ] ) .",
    "these extensions are based on strongly separable algebras , and they are well behaved under tangle composition .",
    "already the simplest example in characteristic @xmath0 ( example  [ ex_barnatan ] ) carries a filtration sophisticated enough to recover our tangle extension of characteristic @xmath0 khovanov homology with all its non - trivial properties ( theorem  [ thm_spectral ] and remark  [ rem_chartwo ] below ) .",
    "the tangle homology presented in this article then has the following desirable properties :    1 .",
    "the tangle homology behaves well with respect to composition .",
    "it respects the monoidal structure of the category of tangles .",
    "it is rich enough to recover the finite characteristic khovanov homology for links as well as rasmussen s @xmath162-invariant .",
    "our use of open - closed tqfts in order to define a tangle homology theory is by no means the most general conceivable approach .",
    "for example , in an open - closed tqft , all the open - closed cobordisms displayed in   have algebraic operations associated with them although only the composites displayed in   to   below are needed in order to define the chain complexes .",
    "this is in analogy to the observation that in khovanov s link homology theory , the unit and counit of the commutative frobenius algebra are not needed to define the chain complex .",
    "notice , however , that both bar - natan s  @xcite and our proof ( section  [ sec_reidemeister ] below ) of reidemeister move invariance still need some of the additional cobordisms .",
    "we have chosen to work with open - closed tqfts mainly because the extension of a @xmath0-dimensional tqft to an open - closed tqft is much better understood than the corresponding question for the temperley ",
    "lieb @xmath0-category .",
    "notice also that in any tangle cobordism theory , the object associated with the unknot ,  in our case the homology of the @xmath19-term complex @xmath163 which is just @xmath121 , automatically carries the structure of a commutative frobenius algebra . since we work with open - closed tqfts , the object associated with the arc ,  the identity tangle on a single point , which is the homology of @xmath164 and thereby just @xmath1 , forms a symmetric frobenius algebra .",
    "this is sufficient to yield an algebraic model for the temperley ",
    "lieb @xmath0-category , but presumably not necessary .",
    "in this section , we introduce the notion of a knowledgeable frobenius algebra .",
    "this is the algebraic structure that is needed to classify open - closed tqfts .",
    "we then summarize the definitions and the main properties of the commutative and anti - commutative cubes of graded and filtered vector spaces that are used to define khovanov s , lee s and bar - natan s chain complexes .",

    ", gluing two open - closed cobordisms along a circle has the following effect . for simplicity suppose that as a cell complex the circle is constructed from a single vertex and a single edge .",
    "then gluing along this circle reduces the number of vertices by one and the number of edges by one , and so it leaves the euler characteristic unchanged .",
    "second , gluing two open - closed cobordisms along an arc with the simplest cell structure has the following effect .",
    "it reduces the number of vertices by two and the number of edges by one , and so it reduces the euler characteristic by one .",
    "the claim holds because at the same time the gluing reduces @xmath385 by two .",
    "if two pairs of disjoint arcs of @xmath102 are joined by the gluing , @xmath386 is reduced by two . if the gluing does not join two disjoint arcs , but rather the two ends of a single arc of @xmath102 , then @xmath387 is unchanged , but @xmath378 increases .",

    "the following definition and theorem are the main results of this section .",
    "they improve bar - natan s result of  @xcite and yield for every tangle ( not just for every link ) a complex of _ vector spaces _ that is invariant under reidemeister moves up to homotopy equivalence .",
    "[ def_tanglecomplex ] let @xmath90 be a plane diagram of an oriented tangle with @xmath7 positive and @xmath9 negative crossings , @xmath11 , let @xmath946 denote a checkerboard colouring of @xmath90 , and let @xmath118 be an euler - graded [ euler - filtered ] open - closed tqft .",

    "[ thm_reidemeister ] let @xmath1008 be plane diagrams of oriented tangles , @xmath946 , and @xmath118 be an euler - graded [ euler - filtered ] open - closed tqft that satisfies bar - natan s conditions .",
    "if @xmath90 and @xmath1009 are related by a reidemeister move or by a plane isotopy , then the complexes @xmath983 and @xmath1010 are homotopy equivalent as graded [ filtered ] complexes .",
    "the proof is almost the same as bar - natan s  @xcite , except that whenever bar - natan writes down a @xmath0-manifold with corners , we apply the open - closed tqft and turn it into a linear map between vector space .",
    "we do not reproduce the proof here .",
    "we do , however , present the proofs for the invariance under reidemeister moves up to homotopy equivalence when we develop the composition operation for tangles in section  [ sec_composition ] below .    1 .",
    "while the commutative cube @xmath966 did not depend on the orientation of the tangle , the tangle complex @xmath983 does depend on it via the grading shift by @xmath1011 and the homological degree shift by @xmath1012 .",
    "these shifts correspond to the prefactor @xmath1013 , @xmath389 , which turns the kauffman bracket into an invariant under ambient isotopy , and they are needed to prove theorem  [ thm_reidemeister ] .",
    "since we have been able to translate from topology to algebra right in the beginning and since @xmath372 and @xmath373 are abelian categories , there is no need to consider formal linear combinations of surfaces as in  @xcite .",

  "abstract_text": [
    "<S> we use a special kind of @xmath0-dimensional extended topological quantum field theories ( tqfts ) , so - called open - closed tqfts , in order to extend khovanov homology from links to arbitrary tangles , not necessarily even . for every plane diagram of an oriented tangle , </S>",
    "<S> we construct a chain complex whose homology is invariant under reidemeister moves . </S>",
    "<S> the terms of this chain complex are modules of a suitable algebra @xmath1 such that there is one action of @xmath1 or @xmath2 for every boundary point of the tangle . </S>",
    "<S> we give examples of such algebras @xmath1 for which our tangle homology theory reduces to the link homology theories of khovanov , lee , and bar - natan if it is evaluated for links . as a consequence of the cardy condition , khovanov s graded theory </S>",
    "<S> can only be extended to tangles if the underlying field has finite characteristic . in all cases </S>",
    "<S> in which the algebra @xmath1 is strongly separable ,  for bar - natan s theory in any characteristic and for lee s theory in characteristic other than @xmath0 , we also provide the required algebraic operation for the composition of oriented tangles . just as khovanov </S>",
    "<S> s theory for links can be recovered from lee s or bar - natan s by a suitable spectral sequence , we provide a spectral sequence in order to compute our tangle extension of khovanov s theory from that of bar - natan s or lee s theory . </S>",
    "<S> thus , we provide a tangle homology theory that is locally computable and still strong enough to recover characteristic @xmath3 khovanov homology for links .    </S>",
    "<S> mathematics subject classification ( 2000 ) : 57r56 , 57m99 , 57m25 , 57q45 , 18g60 . </S>"
  ]
